-s_ ldl>t sf]0f (A + B) / (A - B) lqsf]0fldtLo cg'kft (Trigonometric ratios of

dflysf] lrqdf s]Gb| O af6 PsfO j[Tt lvlrPsf] 5 . пғҗPOS= A / пғҗPOQ =пғҗB dfgf}F .

P(cosA, sinA) 
 
 
Q (cos(A +B), sin(A +B))

ca b'/L ;"qaf6, 
 
SQ2 
= {(cos(A +B)-1}2 +{sin(A + B)-0}2  
 
 
= cos2(A +B) вҖ“ 2 cos(A +B). 1 + 12 + sin2(A+ B) 
 
 
= 1 + 1 вҖ“ 2 cos (A + B) 
 
 
= 2 вҖ“ 2 cos (A + B) 
 
 
= 2{1-cos (A + B)} 
 
To:t}, 
 
PR2 
 = [(cosA вҖ“ cos(-B))2 + (sinA вҖ“ sin(-B))2] 
 
 
= (cosA - cosB)2 + (sinA + sinB)2 
 
 
= cos2A вҖ“ 2cosA cosB + cos2B + sin2A + 2sinA sinB + sin2B 
 
 
= cos2A + sin2A + cos2B + sin2B -2 [cosA cosB вҖ“ sinA sinB] 
 
 
= 1 + 1 -2[cosA cosB вҖ“ sinA sinB]

170 
 
 
= 2 -2[cosA cosB вҖ“ sinA sinB] 
 
 
= 2[1- (cosA cosB-sinA sinB)]

cyjf, 2{1- cos(A +B)] = 2[ 1- (cosA cosB вҖ“ sinA sin B) 
 
 
cyjf, cos(A +B)  
= cosA cosB вҖ“ sinA sin B 
 
 
 
 / cos (A-B)  
= cos{A +(-B)} 
 
 
 
 
 
= cosA.cos(-B) - sinA.sin(-B) 
 
 
 
 
 
= CosA.CosB + SinA.SinB 
 
 
ca, sin(A +B)  
= cos [90  вҖ“(A +B)] 
 
 
 
 
 
= cos [(90  вҖ“A) вҖ“B]
